RM fan here. Real should really be ashamed of themselves, the last time they have beat Barcelona by more than 2 goals difference has been in 2008, 14 years ago. Imagine how bad Barcelona was in the first clasico of the season yet Real still barely won 2-1 with lucky goals (the same last season despite being 2-0 at half time), yet Barca has beaten Real 0-3, 5-1, 0-4 not only now but even during the seasons when Real won the 3 UCLs back to back.   In the case of that first clasico of this season, had the roles ben reversed i.e Real being in crisis and weak and Barca coming from a winning streak and having great players, i'm sure Barca would have won it by at least 11-0. Idk what's the cause here, Real are probably still traumatised from Pep's barca and psychologically don't believe themselves as superiors to Barca anymore no matter which players they face.   From all of these past 10+ years, one can only conclude that Real Madrid is obviously the best team of all the others in history yet head-to-head Real was, is and will be for some time at least 3 levels below Barcelona.   5 clasicos won by 1 or 2 goals difference is nothing compared to countless humiliations over the years including those at santiago bernabeu, including times when Real had much better players. Beyond shameful. Another pretty sad stat is, i can't even remember a season where Barca won the league by losing both clasicos to Real yet Real won the league in 2017 (and champions league too) while losing to Barca in both of the 2 clasicos they had that year.

TAM BÄ°R   HAKSIZLIK YAPILARAK OYUNDU SAOL BAR  SAOL HAKEM
Yilan County Council in Taiwan passed a cross-party motion on December 24 to support the Universal Declaration on Combating and Preventing Forced Organ Harvesting (UDCPFOH). The motion condemns the organ harvesting by the Chinese Communist Party (CCP) and urges the Taiwan government to implement laws to help end the atrocity.    Chang Chiu-ming, a member of Yilan County Council, said a motion was passed on December 24 against organ harvesting.   When the 76th United Nations General Assembly took place in New York in September 2021, five nongovernmental organizations from the US, Europe, and Asia issued UDCPFOH on September 26, the last day of the World Summit on Combating and Preventing Forced Organ Harvesting.   UDCPFOH has been supported by parliament members, government officials, and leaders from many countries. They include Changrok Soh, member of UN Human Rights Council, and Thierry Valle, director of European Federation for Freedom of Belief. It was also endorsed by Arthur Caplan, professor of bioethics at New York University and the founding director of the Medical Ethics Division.   The Taiwan Falun Gong Human Rights Working Group has since contacted the central government as well as county-level governments in Taiwan, urging them to support this initiative. The Group believes that by raising awareness to the general public and taking further actions, leaders from around the world can stop the CCPâ€™s organ harvesting through joint efforts.   During an ad hoc session held by Yilan County Council on December 24, the motion was initiated by three council members including Zhang Chiu-ming, Chen Han-chung, and Tsai Chin-hui. To fulfill its human rights commitment, the motion aims to support the UDCPFOH, condemn the organ harvesting atrocity by the CCP, and institute related criminal legislation. For specific implementation of this resolution, the council requests the county government to contact relevant agencies of the Taiwan Executive Yuan. With 25 cosponsors, including Wu Hong-mo and Yang Tree, this motion was passed in the council.   Chang said he was happy to see Yilan Council supporting the upright with this motion. Yang pointed out the CCPâ€™s brutality of organ harvesting is anti-humanity and it is a disgrace to mankind. He hopes such efforts will stop the atrocity and promote kindness as well as traditional values in society.

As a madrid fan, the state of things right now is simply that Ancelotti has created a place where there is no place for competition. He has no ideology, tactically he's subpar, makes poor substitutions, unable to unify a whole squad of 25 or so players and simply doesn't show any creativity, ingenuity or any sign of commitment to a style of play. It's absolutely ludicrous that 2 missing players could destabilise a whole team so much and yet the evidence was there and i for sure know if mendy and benzema had played the game would have been more competitive but it shouldn't have to be that way. Even dembele with all his drama got a chance to prove his worth with a manager that clearly understands the philosophy and football of his club. In less time xavi has done what i was hoping Ancelotti would do which is make madrid PLAY AS A TEAM instead of constantly relying on moments of individual brilliance by one player. I'm guessing he basically tells the team to stay in the game and vini and rodrygo to run at the opposition and hope for the best. There is no unity in pressing, no players making run behind when a player has the ball, no teamwork of any sort except when they pass simply because they have to. The result was not even the worst part because honestly it didn't really shock me, neither the performance because honestly that's been pretty on par for how we have performed all season but Curtois. For me Ancelotti needs to go at the end of the season, regardless of what players we sign, we cannot have them be managed and ran into the ground by that old dinosaur. His time is passed. Say what you want about mourinho but he will play young players that work hard and we would definitely have more competition in the squad than we do with Ancelotti. Mourinho will play who will get him the results he wants playing the way he wants. Any player that comes into the team will play the way he wants. He has his style, he has plan b to z and even he's considered past it so how can former manager of Everton Ancelotti be manager of Madrid?
